08552 
08553 WCHAR ff_convert (  /* Converted code, 0 means conversion error */
08554     WCHAR   src,    /* Character code to be converted */
08555     UINT    dir     /* 0: Unicode to OEMCP, 1: OEMCP to Unicode */
08556 )
08557 {
08558     const WCHAR *p;
08559     WCHAR c;
08560     int i, n, li, hi;
08561 
08562 
08563     if (src < 0x80) {   /* ASCII */
08564         c = src;
08565     } else {
08566         if (dir) {      /* OEMCP to unicode */
08567             p = oem2uni;
08568             hi = sizeof(oem2uni) / 4 - 1;
08569         } else {        /* Unicode to OEMCP */
08570             p = uni2oem;
08571             hi = sizeof(uni2oem) / 4 - 1;
08572         }
08573         li = 0;
08574         for (n = 16; n; n--) {
08575             i = li + (hi - li) / 2;
08576             if (src == p[i * 2]) break;
08577             if (src > p[i * 2])
08578                 li = i;
08579             else
08580                 hi = i;
08581         }
08582         c = n ? p[i * 2 + 1] : 0;
08583     }
08584 
08585     return c;
08586 }
